		MLW_eco_cleanups = {
			MLW_eco_set_up_skimmer = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {
					check_variable = { MLW_skimmers_set_up < 4 }
					# has_completed_focus = MLW_avoid_backlash
				}
				available = { MLW_not_doing_cleanups = yes }
				custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { treasury > 0.499 } }
				custom_cost_text = cost_0_5
				days_remove = 30
				complete_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.5 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
					set_country_flag = MLW_eco_cleanups_occuring
				}
				remove_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { DM_health_cost_change = -0.025 }
					update_MLW_lakeside_healthcare_cost = yes
					add_to_variable = { MLW_skimmers_set_up = 1 }
					clr_country_flag = MLW_eco_cleanups_occuring
				}
			}
			MLW_eco_ban_dumping = {

			MLW_LW_shared_border_corrections = {
				icon = decision
				visible = { MLW_LW_border_correction_visible_check = yes }
				available = {}

				cost = 50

				days_remove = 30
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = MLW_LW_diplomatic_FLAG

						limit = { check_variable = { ROOT.MLW_LW_state_selected = 1045.id } }
						TNZ = { country_event = MLW_FOPOL_LW.1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { ROOT.MLW_LW_state_selected = 1049.id } }

					}
				}
				remove_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { MLW_LW_progress_change = 1 }
					MLW_LW_update_diplomatic_progress = yes

			}
			MLW_LW_city_twinning = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {}
				available = { MLW_LW_city_twinning_available_check = yes }

				cost = 50

				days_remove = 30
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = MLW_LW_diplomatic_FLAG
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -2 }

						limit = {
							OR = {
								MLW_LW_MBEYA = yes
								MLW_LW_NJOMBE = yes
								MLW_LW_WESTRUVUMA = yes
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = TNZ }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = MLW }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = MLW }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TNZ }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_LW_MBEYA = yes }
							1045 = { set_state_flag = MLW_LW_twinned_city }
							newline = yes
							custom_effect_tooltip = MLW_LW_mbeya_twin_TT
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_LW_NJOMBE = yes }
							1046 = { set_state_flag = MLW_LW_twinned_city }
							newline = yes
							custom_effect_tooltip = MLW_LW_njombe_twin_TT
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_LW_WESTRUVUMA = yes }
							1047 = { set_state_flag = MLW_LW_twinned_city }
							newline = yes
							custom_effect_tooltip = MLW_LW_westruvuma_twin_TT
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { MLW_LW_WESTNIASSA = yes }
						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = MOZ }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = MLW }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = MLW }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = MOZ }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
						newline = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = MLW_LW_westniassa_twin_TT
						1049 = { set_state_flag = MLW_LW_twinned_city }
					}
				}
				remove_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { MLW_LW_progress_change = 2 }
					MLW_LW_update_diplomatic_progress = yes
					clr_country_flag = MLW_LW_diplomatic_FLAG
				}
			}

							set_border_war_data = {
								attacker = 1049
								defender = 1047
								defender_modifier = MLW_LW_defence_VAR
							}
						}
					}
					if = { # WEST NIASSA - 1049
						limit = { MLW_LW_WESTNIASSA = yes }
						if = { # FROM SOUTH MALAWI - 260
							limit = { has_country_flag = MLW_LW_assault_launched_from_SOUTH_MALAWI }
							start_border_war = {
								change_state_after_war = no
								attacker = {
									state = 260
									num_provinces = 1
									on_win = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.70
									on_lose = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.71
									on_cancel = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.7
								}
								defender = {
									state = 1049
									num_provinces = 1
									on_win = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.70
									on_lose = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.71
									on_cancel = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.7
								}
							}
							set_border_war_data = {
								attacker = 260
								defender = 1049
								defender_modifier = MLW_LW_defence_VAR
							}
						}
						if = { # FROM WEST RUVUMA - 1047
							limit = { has_country_flag = MLW_LW_assault_launched_from_WEST_RUVUMA }
							start_border_war = {
								change_state_after_war = no
								attacker = {
									state = 1047
									num_provinces = 1
									on_win = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.80
									on_lose = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.81
									on_cancel = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.8
								}
								defender = {
									state = 1049
									num_provinces = 1
									on_win = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.80
									on_lose = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.81
									on_cancel = MLW_FOPOL_LWBW.8
								}
							}
							set_border_war_data = {
								attacker = 1049
								defender = 1047
								defender_modifier = MLW_LW_defence_VAR
							}
						}
					}
				}

	# MLW-ZAM JPCC
		MLW_ZAM_JPCC = {
			MLW_JPCC_conferences = {
				icon = decision
				visible = { has_completed_focus = MLW_ZAM_maintain_JPCC }
				available = { MLW_JPCC_conferences_not_underway = yes }
				custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 9 }
				custom_cost_text = command_power_more_than_10
				days_remove = 14
				days_re_enable = 120
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = { flag = MLW_JPCC_conferences_held days = 180 value = 1 }
					add_command_power = -10
				}
				remove_effect = {
					hidden_effect = {
						random_list = {
							10 = { set_country_flag = MLW_JPCC_whoopsie_CON }
							80 = { set_country_flag = MLW_JPCC_business_as_usual_CON }
							10 = { set_country_flag = MLW_JPCC_were_the_best_alliance_CON }
						}
						country_event = MLW_FOPOL_ZAM.4
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = MLW_JPCC_conferences_TT
				}
			}

			MLW_rail_to_MOZ = {
				icon = decision
				fire_only_once = yes
				visible = {
					OR = {

						is_debug = yes
					}
				}
				available = {
					MOZ = {
						has_opinion = {
							target = MLW
							value > 49
						}
					}
				}
				custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { treasury > 1.59 } }
				custom_cost_text = MLW_rails_1_6
				days_remove = 14
				complete_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -1.6 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes

				remove_effect = {
					MOZ = { country_event = MLW_rails.1 }
					newline = yes
					set_temp_variable = { accept_tag = MOZ }

					effect_tooltip = {
						build_railway = {
							level = 1
							path = { 5155 12935 11363 5177 }
						}
					}
					newline = yes
				}
			}

		MLW_privatisation_decision_CAT = {
			MLW_UDF_privatisation_IND = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = MLW_UDF_privatisation
						is_debug = yes
					}
				}
				available = {
					MLW_privatisation_interest_rate = yes
					MLW_privatisation_treasury_contents = yes
					industrial_complex > 1
					MLW_privatisation_underway = yes
				}
				cost = 25
				days_remove = 180
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = {
						flag = MLW_privatisation_underway_flag
						value = 1
						days = 180
					}
				}
				remove_effect = {
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = { industrial_complex > 0 }
						remove_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
						}
						set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 11.25 }
						modify_treasury_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
			MLW_UDF_privatisation_MIL = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = MLW_UDF_privatisation
						is_debug = yes
					}
				}
				available = {
					MLW_privatisation_interest_rate = yes
					MLW_privatisation_treasury_contents = yes
					arms_factory > 1
					MLW_privatisation_underway = yes
				}
				cost = 25
				days_remove = 180
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = {
						flag = MLW_privatisation_underway_flag
						value = 1
						days = 180
					}
				}
				remove_effect = {
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
						remove_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
						}
						set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 11.25 }
						modify_treasury_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
			MLW_UDF_privatisation_DOC = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = MLW_UDF_privatisation
						is_debug = yes
					}
				}
				available = {
					MLW_privatisation_interest_rate = yes
					MLW_privatisation_treasury_contents = yes
					dockyard > 1
					MLW_privatisation_underway = yes
				}
				cost = 25
				days_remove = 180
				complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = {
						flag = MLW_privatisation_underway_flag
						value = 1
						days = 180
					}
				}
				remove_effect = {
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = { dockyard > 0 }
						remove_building = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
						}
						set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 11.25 }
						modify_treasury_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
			MLW_UDF_privatisation_OFF = {
				icon = decision
				visible = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = MLW_UDF_privatisation
						is_debug = yes

				available = {
